**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

   - `pkg/services/grpcserver/interceptors/auth.go` - gRPC authentication using API keys

## API Key Authentication and Scope Enforcement in Grafana

### Core Files Found

| File | Role |
|------|------|
| `pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go` | **Primary auth client** — validates API keys, checks expiration/revocation/org-scope |
| `pkg/services/apikey/apikey.go` | Service interface definition |
| `pkg/services/apikey/model.go` | Data model (`APIKey` struct with `Expires`, `IsRevoked`, `OrgID`) |
| `pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/apikey.go` | Service implementation |
| `pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/store.go` | Store interface |
| `pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/xorm_store.go` | Database store (key lookup, expiration storage, last-used updates) |
| `pkg/services/contexthandler/contexthandler.go` | HTTP middleware entry point that triggers authentication |
| `pkg/middleware/auth.go` | Scope/role enforcement middleware (`Auth()`, `RoleAuth()`) |
| `pkg/middleware/middleware.go` | Pre-built middleware instances (`ReqSignedIn`, `ReqOrgAdmin`) |
| `pkg/services/grpcserver/interceptors/auth.go` | gRPC API key authentication |
| `pkg/components/satokengen/tokengen.go` | New `gl`-prefixed token generation/decoding |
| `pkg/components/apikeygen/apikeygen.go` | Legacy base64 API key generation/decoding |

### Key Authentication Chain
1. `ContextHandler.Middleware()` → `setRequestContext()` → `authenticator.Authenticate()`
2. → `APIKey.Authenticate()` → `getTokenFromRequest()` → `getAPIKey()`
3. → `validateApiKey()` — checks **expiration** (`Expires <= now`), **revocation** (`IsRevoked`), **org scope** (`orgID != key.OrgID`), and **service account linkage**
4. → Route handlers apply `Auth()`, `ReqSignedIn`, `ReqOrgAdmin` for additional scope enforcement

<token>` and `Basic api_key:<token>` formats).\\n- `getAPIKey()`: Dispatches to `getFromToken()` (for new `gl`-prefixed service account tokens) or `getFromTokenLegacy()` (for old base64-encoded keys).\\n- `validateApiKey()`: **Key scope/expiration enforcement** \u2014 checks that the key has not expired (`key.Expires <= time.Now().Unix()`), is not revoked (`key.IsRevoked`), belongs to the requested organization (`orgID != key.OrgID`), and is linked to a service account.\\n- `Hook()`: Post-authentication hook that asynchronously updates the key's `last_used_at` timestamp.\\n- `shouldUpdateLastUsedAt()`: Throttles last-used updates to once per 5 minutes.\\n\\n## API Key Service Layer\\n\\n**`pkg/services/apikey/apikey.go`** defines the `Service` interface with methods: `ContextHandler.Middleware()` \u2014 the HTTP middleware that wraps every request. Its `setRequestContext()` method calls `h.authenticator.Authenticate()`, which routes to the `APIKey` client when a Bearer/Basic token is present. It decodes the Bearer token using `satokengen.Decode()`, looks up the key by hash, verifies the linked service account has Admin role, and checks that the account is not disabled.\\n\\n## Token Generation/Decoding\\n\\n**`pkg/components/satokengen/tokengen.go`** implements the new `gl`-prefixed service account token format: `New()` generates tokens, `Decode()` parses and validates the checksum, and `Hash()` produces the stored hash.\\n\\n**`pkg/components/apikeygen/apikeygen.go`** implements the legacy base64-encoded API key format: `New()` generates keys, `Decode()` parses them, and `IsValid()` validates the HMAC.\\n\\n## Authentication Flow\\n\\n1.
